	}

	}

				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
		}
		CZE_subtract_three_collapse = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeczeflavor.4
				days = 7
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
}
